info:Superior 2-bed Room

info:Family
info:24 Reviews
rating:4.5
posted:Posted October 6, 2023
msg:A five-star hotel in the southwest corner of Shenyang, but the price is very reasonable during the National Day.
After on-site experience, I feel that there are pros and cons.
The advantages are: the price is right, there are thousands of hotels in the National Games Village to the east, and there are only half of them here. This is the core advantage; the service is in place, call in advance to inquire; the room is in line with five-star standards, with a large area, a bathtub, and free fruit.
The disadvantage is: construction in the gate area can only be done from the side. It may be related to the thunderstorm in Country Garden. It feels like no one is working on it. It may be like this for a long time, giving it a sense of dilapidation. There is no swimming pool, billiards or anything else is not open. Parking is also difficult.
